snying thig sngon 'gro'i khrid yig thar lam gsal byed dang lam bzang ye shes snying po bcas bzhugs so/_/

ye shes snying po bcas 
bzhugs so/_/
rig 'dzin 'gro 'dul dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad/
rdza 'gyur dpe tshogs/

/a 'dzoms 'brug pa rin po che 'gro 'dul dpa' bo rdo rje mchog ni/

dka'i dal ba thob gyur kyang /_/skad cig mi rtag 'gyur ba'i chos can te/_/rnam 
par brtags na snying po 'ga' med pas/_/lbu ba rdos 'dra yid rton mi rung bas/_/
nyin mtshan kun tu nges par 'chi ba soms/_/zhes pa ltar/_dang po phyi snod kyi 'jig 
rten la bsam nas mi rtag pa sgom pa ni/_'di ltar 'gro ba spyi mthun gyi bsod nams 
las grub pa'i phyi snod kyi 'jig rten gling bzhi ri rab lha gnas dang bcas pa sra zhing 
'thas pa bskal pa'i bar du gnas pa 'di dag kyang mthar me bdun chu gcig gis 
'jig cing mi rtag par 'gyur ba can yin te/_de nyid las/_snod bcud mi rtag 
srid pa chags 'jig gis/_/me bdun chu gcig rlung gis gtor ba'i tshe/_/khor 
yug rin chen gling dang ris bskor ba'i/_/lhun po rin chen gzhi yang mi rtag cing /_/
thams cad nam mkha' gcig tu 'gyur ba'i skabs/_/nges par soms la snying nas 
chos mdzod cig_/ces so/_/gnyis pa/_nang bcud kyi sems can mi rtag pa sgom 
pa ni/_'di ltar srid pa'i rtse mo nas dmyal ba'i gnas yan chad na sems can yod 
do cog 'chi ba'i gnas las thar ba ni gcig kyang med la/_dper na sa steng gi 
'gro ba mi la mtshon na/_de ring nyi ma 'di yan chod mi lo brgya'i gong rol nas skyes 
pa'i 'dzam bu gling gi mi mchog dman bar ma brtsi ba'i tshad las 'das pa zhig byung 
ba yang da lta ming gi lhag ma tsam las gcig kyang med/_sngon las sam tshe sgrub pa'i

mkha' la gza' skar ltar bkra zhing*/_/'gro kun phan bde'i dpal yon rdzogs 
ldan dus ston zla bor gong nas gong 'phel te/_/mi mthun phyogs las rnam par 
rgyal zhing bkra shis snang ba dam pa rtag 'char shog_/ces 'od gsal sprul pa'i rdo 
rje'i zhal snga nas lce btsun snying thig gi khyad par gyi khrid yig go sla gnad 'dus 
shig bris shig ces pa'i bka' lung dang /_byang gter bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan zur 
chen chos dbyings rang grol gyi yang srid/_mkhyen brtse ye shes rdo rje'i sku sras thub 
bstan rdo rje brag gi mkhan zur dam pa bsod nams rnam rgyal pas dgongs pa zang 
thal thun mong thun min khyad par gyi khrid yig go sla gnad 'dus zhig bri dgos 
zhes/_dngos rdzas phyag ring brkyangs pa'i gnang spyin lan gsum bar rgya chen 
bcas bskul ba dang /_lam 'di la mos pa che ba sgrub brtson pad+ma rgyal mtshan gyis 
gu ru seng+ge'i sgra sgrogs zangs gser can gyi 'dra 'bag gi skyes bcas lce btsun 
snying thig gi khyad par gyi khrid yig 'dri dgos tshul bskul bas rkyen byas/_da lta 
rang dang lam 'di la mos pa rnams dang /_ma 'ongs skal ldan rnams kyi gdams 
ngag gi lam mi nor ba'i brjed byang lta bu la dmigs te/_ris med rgyal bstan 
spyi dang lam 'di sogs kun gyi gral mthar 'khod pa rig 'dzin sna tshogs rang 
grol rtsal du 'bod pa'i gdol spyod pa des rang lo drug cu rtsa dgur son pa'i 
lcags khyi ston zla ra ba/_lce btsun seng+ge dbang phyug 'od phung du gshegs pa'i tshes 
bcu'i dus mchod nyin rdzogs par bris pa'i yi ge'i 'du byed rang slob skal bzang 
zla ba rgyal mtshan gyis bgyis te/_rang gnas bkra shis dung dkar 'khyil 'dri'i 
ri zhol 'od gsal theg mchod gling nas legs par spel bas smon pa'i gnas 
kun de de bzhin du 'grub par gyur cig_/_//

#/_/khrid yig lam bzang_ye shes snying po/
!yig sgrig dang rtsis 'phrul pa/_re skong 'jigs med bshad sgrub/
zhu dag pa/_gser grwa thub bstan ye shes/
'jigs med bshad sgrub/

#/_/rig 'dzin 'gro 'dul[¸\u0f7a]dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad/
yi ge nyi shu rtsa drug pa 'di dpe cha'i nang du bzhag na dpe cha der ci 'drar 
bgoms kyang nyes pa mi 'byung bar 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud las gsungs so/

#/_/ston pa'i dam chos rnam gnyis te/_/
lung dang rtogs pa'i bdag nyid do/_/
de 'dzin byed pa smra byed dang*/_/
